<p><strong>Features</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Built with flexbox for flexible layout and SSR</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports horizontal and vertical panels</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports multiple panels and resize handles</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports collapsible panels</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports panel constraints like min and max sizes</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Programmatic control of panel sizes</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Implements the
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/windowsplitter/" class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px">Window Splitter pattern</a>
for accessibility and keyboard controls</li>
</ul>

<p>Check the splitter anatomy and part names.</p>

<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the splitter package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> splitter</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/splitter&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>The splitter package exports two key functions:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - State machine logic.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
</ul>
<p>Then use the framework integration helpers:</p>
<div data-scope="tabs" data-part="root" id="tabs:splitter/usage.mdx" data-orientation="horizontal" dir="ltr" class="w_full max-w_768px bd-w_1px my_8 bg_bg.code.block bdr_6px"><div data-scope="tabs" </span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token language-javascript"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getRootProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>

<h3 id="setting-the-initial-size" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting the initial size<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-initial-size"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To set the initial size of the splitter panels, use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultSize</code> property.
Ensure the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultSize</code> totals to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">100</code>.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Note: The splitter only supports setting percentage values.</p>
</blockquote>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>splitter<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// ...</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">defaultSize</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">40</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">60</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="controlled-panel-sizes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlled panel sizes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlled-panel-sizes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">size</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onResize</code> for controlled layouts.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>splitter<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">setSize</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">size</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-for-resize-events" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for resize events<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-resize-events"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the resize trigger is dragged, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onResize</code>, <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onResizeStart</code> and
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onResizeEnd</code> callbacks are invoked.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>splitter<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>

<h3 id="changing-the-orientation" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Changing the orientation<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#changing-the-orientation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>By default, the splitter is assumed to be horizontal. To change the orientation
to vertical, set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">orientation</code> property in the machine&#x27;s context to
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">vertical</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>splitter<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// ...</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">orientation</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;vertical&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="specifying-constraints" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Specifying constraints<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#specifying-constraints"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">panels</code> property to specify constraints like <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">minSize</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">maxSize</code>
for the splitter panels.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>splitter<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// ...</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">panels</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;a&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">minSize</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">maxSize</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">80</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;b&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">minSize</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">maxSize</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">80</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="configuring-keyboard-resize-step" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Configuring keyboard resize step<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#configuring-keyboard-resize-step"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">keyboardResizeBy</code> to control how many pixels arrow keys resize by.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>splitter<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  panels<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">keyboardResizeBy</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">16</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="setting-the-collapsed-size" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting the collapsed size<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-collapsed-size"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">collapsedSize</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">collapsible</code> of a panel to specify the collapsed
size of the panel.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>For best results, ensure you also set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">minSize</code> of the panel</p>
</blockquote>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>splitter<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// ...</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">panels</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;a&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">collapsible</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">collapsedSize</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">5</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">minSize</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">maxSize</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">20</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;b&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">minSize</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">50</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>This allows the user to drag the splitter to collapse the panel to the
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">collapsedSize</code>.</p>
<h3 id="listening-for-collapse-events" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for collapse events<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-collapse-events"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the splitter panel is collapsed, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onCollapse</code> callback is invoked.
Alternatively, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onExpand</code> callback is invoked when the panel is expanded.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>splitter<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// ...</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">onCollapse</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">detail</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;collapse&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> detail<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">onExpand</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">detail</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;expand&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> detail<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="programmatic-panel-control" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Programmatic panel control<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#programmatic-panel-control"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use the connected API to resize, collapse, or expand panels from code.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">setSizes</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">30</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">70</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">resizePanel</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;a&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">40</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">collapsePanel</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;a&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">expandPanel</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;a&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<h3 id="resize-trigger" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Resize trigger<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#resize-trigger"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When a resize trigger is horizontal or vertical, a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-orientation</code> attribute
is set on the trigger element.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;splitter&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;resize-trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the item */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;splitter&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;resize-trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-orientation</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;horizontal&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the item is horizontal state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;splitter&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;resize-trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-orientation</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;vertical&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the item is horizontal state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;splitter&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;resize-trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-focus</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the item is focus state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;splitter&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;resize-trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token pseudo-class">:active</span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>The splitter&#x27;s <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods and properties:</p>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The splitter machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">orientation</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;horizontal&quot; | &quot;vertical&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The orientation of the splitter. Can be `horizontal` or `vertical`</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">size</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number[]</code><span class="d_block">The controlled size data of the panels</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultSize</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number[]</code><span class="d_block">The initial size of the panels when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the size of the panels.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">panels</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">PanelData[]</code><span class="d_block">The size constraints of the panels.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onResize</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: ResizeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the splitter is resized.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onResizeStart</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the splitter resize starts.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onResizeEnd</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: ResizeEndDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the splitter resize ends.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ root: string; resizeTrigger: (id: string) =&gt; string; label: (id: string) =&gt; string; panel: (id: string | number) =&gt; string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the elements in the splitter. Useful for composition.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">keyboardResizeBy</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The number of pixels to resize the panel by when the keyboard is used.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">nonce</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The nonce for the injected splitter cursor stylesheet.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onCollapse</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: ExpandCollapseDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when a panel is collapsed.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onExpand</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: ExpandCollapseDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when a panel is expanded.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dir</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;ltr&quot; | &quot;rtl&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The document&#x27;s text/writing direction.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The unique identifier of the machine.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getRootNode</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; ShadowRoot | Node | Document</code><span class="d_block">A root node to correctly resolve document in custom environments. E.x.: Iframes, Electron.</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The splitter <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dragging</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the splitter is currently being resized.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">orientation</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;horizontal&quot; | &quot;vertical&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The orientation of the splitter.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getSizes</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; number[]</code><span class="d_block">Returns the current sizes of the panels.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">setSizes</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(size: number[]) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Sets the sizes of the panels.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getItems</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; SplitterItem[]</code><span class="d_block">Returns the items of the splitter.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getPanels</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; PanelData</code><span class="d_block">Returns the panel with the specified id.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getPanelSize</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(id: string) =&gt; number</code><span class="d_block">Returns the size of the specified panel.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">isPanelCollapsed</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(id: string) =&gt; boolean</code><span class="d_block">Returns whether the specified panel is collapsed.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">isPanelExpanded</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(id: string) =&gt; boolean</code><span class="d_block">Returns whether the specified panel is expanded.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">collapsePanel</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(id: string) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Collapses the specified panel.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">expandPanel</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(id: string, minSize?: number) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Expands the specified panel.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">resizePanel</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(id: string, unsafePanelSize: number) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Resizes the specified panel.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getLayout</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; string</code><span class="d_block">Returns the layout of the splitter.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">resetSizes</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">VoidFunction</code><span class="d_block">Resets the splitter to its initial state.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getResizeTriggerState</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(props: ResizeTriggerProps) =&gt; ResizeTriggerState</code><span class="d_block">Returns the state of the resize trigger.</span></li></ul>

likely forgot to import, pass, or provide it.\")}"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"12:T14aa,"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"A splitter creates resizable layouts with horizontal or vertical panels.\n\n\u003cResources pkg=\"@zag-js/splitter\" /\u003e\n\n\u003cShowcase id=\"Splitter\" /\u003e\n\n**Features**\n\n- Built with flexbox for flexible layout and SSR\n- Supports horizontal and vertical panels\n- Supports multiple panels and resize handles\n- Supports collapsible panels\n- Supports panel constraints like min and max sizes\n- Programmatic control of panel sizes\n- Implements the\n  [Window Splitter pattern](https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/windowsplitter/)\n  for accessibility and keyboard controls\n\n## Installation\n\nInstall the splitter package:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"splitter/installation.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\nCheck the splitter anatomy and part names.\n\n\u003e Each part includes a `data-part` attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"splitter\" /\u003e\n\n## Usage\n\nImport the splitter package:\n\n```jsx\nimport * as splitter from \"@zag-js/splitter\"\n```\n\nThe splitter package exports two key functions:\n\n- `machine` - State machine logic.\n- `connect` - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\n\nThen use the framework integration helpers:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"splitter/usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Setting the initial size\n\nTo set the initial size of the splitter panels, use the `defaultSize` property.\nEnsure the `defaultSize` totals to `100`.\n\n\u003e Note: The splitter only supports setting percentage values.\n\n```jsx {3}\nconst service = useMachine(splitter.machine, {\n  // ...\n  defaultSize: [40, 60],\n})\n```\n\n### Controlled panel sizes\n\nUse `size` and `onResize` for controlled layouts.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(splitter.machine, {\n  panels,\n  size,\n  onResize(details) {\n    setSize(details.size)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for resize events\n\nWhen the resize trigger is dragged, the `onResize`, `onResizeStart` and\n`onResizeEnd` callbacks are invoked.\n\n```jsx {3-10}\nconst service = useMachine(splitter.machine, {\n  // ...\n  onResize(detail) {\n    console.log(\"resize\", detail)\n  },\n  onResizeStart() {\n    console.log(\"resize start\")\n  },\n  onResizeEnd(detail) {\n    console.log(\"change end\", detail)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Changing the orientation\n\nBy default, the splitter is assumed to be horizontal. To change the orientation\nto vertical, set the `orientation` property in the machine's context to\n`vertical`.\n\n```jsx {3}\nconst service = useMachine(splitter.machine, {\n  // ...\n  orientation: \"vertical\",\n})\n```\n\n## Specifying constraints\n\nUse the `panels` property to specify constraints like `minSize` and `maxSize`\nfor the splitter panels.\n\n```jsx {3-6}\nconst service = useMachine(splitter.machine, {\n  // ...\n  panels: [\n    { id: \"a\", minSize: 20, maxSize: 80 },\n    { id: \"b\", minSize: 20, maxSize: 80 },\n  ],\n})\n```\n\n### Configuring keyboard resize step\n\nUse `keyboardResizeBy` to control how many pixels arrow keys resize by.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(splitter.machine, {\n  panels,\n  keyboardResizeBy: 16,\n})\n```\n\n### Setting the collapsed size\n\nSet the `collapsedSize` and `collapsible` of a panel to specify the collapsed\nsize of the panel.\n\n\u003e For best results, ensure you also set the `minSize` of the panel\n\n```jsx {4}\nconst service = useMachine(splitter.machine, {\n  // ...\n  panels: [\n    { id: \"a\", collapsible: true, collapsedSize: 5, minSize: 10, maxSize: 20 },\n    { id: \"b\", minSize: 50 },\n  ],\n})\n```\n\nThis allows the user to drag the splitter to collapse the panel to the\n`collapsedSize`.\n\n### Listening for collapse events\n\nWhen the splitter panel is collapsed, the `onCollapse` callback is invoked.\nAlternatively, the `onExpand` callback is invoked when the panel is expanded.\n\n```jsx {3-8}\nconst service = useMachine(splitter.machine, {\n  // ...\n  onCollapse(detail) {\n    console.log(\"collapse\", detail)\n  },\n  onExpand(detail) {\n    console.log(\"expand\", detail)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Programmatic panel control\n\nUse the connected API to resize, collapse, or expand panels from code.\n\n```jsx\napi.setSizes([30, 70])\napi.resizePanel(\"a\", 40)\napi.collapsePanel(\"a\")\napi.expandPanel(\"a\")\napi.resetSizes()\n```\n\n## Styling guide\n\nEach part includes a `data-part` attribute you can target in CSS.\n\n### Resize trigger\n\nWhen a resize trigger is horizontal or vertical, a `data-orientation` attribute\nis set on the trigger element.\n\n```css\n[data-scope=\"splitter\"][data-part=\"resize-trigger\"] {\n  /* styles for the item */\n}\n\n[data-scope=\"splitter\"][data-part=\"resize-trigger\"][data-orientation=\"horizontal\"] {\n  /* styles for the item is horizontal state */\n}\n\n[data-scope=\"splitter\"][data-part=\"resize-trigger\"][data-orientation=\"vertical\"] {\n  /* styles for the item is horizontal state */\n}\n\n[data-scope=\"splitter\"][data-part=\"resize-trigger\"][data-focus] {\n  /* styles for the item is focus state */\n}\n\n[data-scope=\"splitter\"][data-part=\"resize-trigger\"]:active {\n  /* styles for the item is active state */\n}\n\n[data-scope=\"splitter\"][data-part=\"resize-trigger\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for the item is disabled state */\n}\n```\n\n## Methods and Properties\n\nThe splitter's `api` exposes the following methods and properties:\n\n### Machine Context\n\nThe splitter machine exposes the following context properties:\n\n\u003cContextTable name=\"splitter\" /\u003e\n\n### Machine API\n\nThe splitter `api` exposes the following methods:\n\n\u003cApiTable name=\"splitter\" /\u003e\n\n### Data Attributes\n\n\u003cDataAttrTable name=\"splitter\" /\u003e"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"5:[\"$\",\"$Le\",null,{\"doc\":{\"title\":\"Splitter\",\"description\":\"Using the splitter machine in your
